The `validate()` block asserts that `sasl.mechanism.inter.broker.protocol` is contained in `sasl.enabled.mechanisms` when SASL is used for inter-broker communication.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/ChannelBuilders.java`: In `serverChannelBuilder()` and the private `create()` method, the server-side code iterates over each mechanism in `BrokerSecurityConfigs.SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG` and calls `JaasContext.loadServerContext()` for each one, triggering JAAS presence validation.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java`: In its constructor (lines 177-186), it validates that `sasl.enabled.mechanisms` is non-null and non-empty, and that a callback handler and Subject exist for every listed mechanism.\\n\\n**2. JAAS config presence check**\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/JaasContext.java`: The `loadServerContext()` method loads or locates the JAAS configuration for each enabled mechanism. `defaultContext()` throws `IllegalArgumentException` with a descriptive message if neither the listener-scoped context name (e.g., `sasl_plaintext.KafkaServer`) nor the global `KafkaServer` entry is found in the JAAS configuration file. The `load()` method validates that the dynamic `sasl.jaas.config` property contains exactly one login module.\\n\\n**3. also triggers `KerberosLogin` via `defaultLoginClass()` and adds native GSS credentials\\n  - OAUTHBEARER → `OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler` (default) or a custom class\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramServerCallbackHandler.java`: Handles SCRAM credential lookup from the broker credential cache.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler.java`: The production OAUTHBEARER validator; `configure()` validates JWKS endpoint URL and JWT validator configuration.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/internals/unsecured/OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler.java`: The default (non-production) OAUTHBEARER validator; its `configure()` checks that exactly one non-null JAAS mechanism entry is provided.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/OAuthBearerLoginCallbackHandler.java`: Validates OAUTHBEARER login configuration including token endpoint URL.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/CommonClientConfigs.java`: `postValidateSaslMechanismConfig()` ensures that when `security.protocol` is `SASL_PLAINTEXT` or `SASL_SSL`, the `sasl.mechanism` is non-null and non-empty.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/internals/BrokerSecurityConfigs.java`: Defines `SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG` and related broker security configuration constants used throughout the validation chain.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":913,"cache_read_input_tokens":92771,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":913,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":10,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"92809cfb-f370-4f65-ad2c-ee20db9f2ba2","uuid":"72b75290-dc44-43a5-b391-4d3fe7a15b9b"}
